, serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The gay side kick of Aristotle wrote : \u201c Orpheus so hated women he chose to be reborn as a motherless swan\u201d&nbsp;&nbsp;.&nbsp;&nbsp;It is a pity that he visited India , yet he knew nothing of Brahmacharya.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">However Plato respects Orpheus for his poetry ,the sweet hymns&nbsp;&nbsp;of the hexameter form that revolutionized Greek poetry.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;For Greek / Latin classics Homer's Iliad and Odyssey and Virgil's Aeneid have inherent the Dactylic hexameter ( heroic hexameter)&nbsp;&nbsp;a form of meter in poetry or a rhythmic scheme, like the metered Sanskrit verses.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The mysterious The Testament of Orpheus was the most important Orphic document for six centuries after it\u2019s \u201cdiscovery\u201d circa 300 AD.&nbsp;&nbsp;In it Orpheus says when in Egypt he met Moses who taught him about monotheism.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A circa 350 AD hematite magic amulet, once in the collection of the Berlin Museum, depicted a man crucified on a cross with a moon and seven stars above his head and the words Orpheoc Bakkikoc.&nbsp;&nbsp;It was declared to be a forgery by a furious pope Pius XII.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">The Orphic doctrine was purely vedic Indian and&nbsp;&nbsp;remained on a mythological plane, interpreting the universe in terms of personalized deities and procreation. Pythagoras refined and rationalized it and grabbed the glory later.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">A Indian Christian trader named Theophilos, from originally from Kerala and resident in Socotra island ( Aloe vera trade ) undertook several missionary journeys on behalf of the Roman emperor Constantius in the mid-4th century.&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;He writes of a small Christian community in on the Malabar coast which traces its origins to Jesus' disciples Thomas and&nbsp;&nbsp;Bartholomew.&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Bartholomew is one of the 12 disciples of Jesus and ismentioned in three Synoptic gospels: Matthew,[10:1\u20134] Mark,[3:13\u201319] and Luke,[6:12\u201316] and also appears as one of the witnesses of the Ascension[Acts 1:4,12,13]; however, each time he is named in the company of Philip.</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">He is not mentioned in Gospel of John.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In the mid-6th century the Alexandrian merchant Kosmas Indikopleustes (India-navigator- TEE HEEEE ) is reputed to have visited the Malabar coast and Ceylon.&nbsp;&nbsp;Kosmas was the author of a stolen world-geography and a book on stolen Kerala astronomy.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">In his letter The Orphic Comparison of the Sun to God Ficino explains \u201cIt is certainly in the Sun that visible light is created from the light of consciousness, and there also sight is created from&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">understanding.&nbsp;&nbsp;For there understanding is no different from the light of consciousness, nor sight from visible light.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">Consciousness ?&nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\">TEEE HEEEE !<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"text-align: left;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; line-height: normal; , serif; font-size: 12pt;\"><br /></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><b><span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">The word 'Vatican' itself is derived from the Sanskrit word Vatika, which means Vedic &nbsp;religious centers, such as Yagna-Vatika. &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></b></span><b style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: red; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He feels he needs to go for a crap , and so he stops at the best motel in town.</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></i></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Meanwhile the motel owner races to the town\u2019s resident whore and returns the 100 dollars he owes her. The whore rushes to the tailor and return 100 dollars she owes him. The tailor rushes to the butcher, the butcher rushes to the tavern owner etc etc\u2014this 100 dollar changes hands several times , before the 100 dollar bill comes back to the motel owner via the local blacksmith who had used the motel several times.&nbsp;</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTP5PaEbGsI/AAAAAAAAC7I/Uw45S0TXvOA/s1600/images+%252858%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTP5PaEbGsI/AAAAAAAAC7I/Uw45S0TXvOA/s1600/images+%252858%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;</div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Recently a batchmate forwarded an interesting article which was written by an Indian Economist to all our batchmates.<br />\n<br />\nJapanese save a lot. They do not spend much. Also, Japan exports far more than it imports. Has an annual trade surplus of over 100 billion. Yet Japanese economy is considered weak, even collapsing.<br />\n<br />\nAmericans spend, save little. Also US imports more than it exports. Has an annual trade deficit of over $400 billion. Yet, the American economy is considered strong and trusted to get stronger.<br />\n<br />\nBut where from do Americans get money to spend? They borrow from Japan , China and even India . Virtually others save for the US to spend. Global savings are mostly invested in US, in dollars.<br />\n<br />\nIndia itself keeps its foreign currency assets of over $50 billion in US securities. China has sunk over $160 billion in US securities.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTQxtMsxNuI/AAAAAAAAC70/bv9SMACL8NE/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTQxtMsxNuI/AAAAAAAAC70/bv9SMACL8NE/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTQxxpQA0RI/AAAAAAAAC74/dAZgvVRxIZI/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTQxxpQA0RI/AAAAAAAAC74/dAZgvVRxIZI/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\nJapan 's stakes in US securities is in trillions.<br />\n<br />\nResult:<br />\n<br />\nThe US has taken over $5 trillion from the world. So, as the world saves for the US - It\u2019s The Americans who spend freely. Today, to keep the US consumption going, that is for the US economy to work, other countries have to remit $180 billion every quarter, which is $2 billion a day, to the US !<br />\n<br />\nA Chinese economist asked a neat question. Who has invested more, US in China , or China in US? The US has invested in China less than half of what China has invested in US.<br />\n<br />\nThe same is the case with India . We have invested in US over $50 billion. But the US has invested less than $20 billion in India .<br />\n<br />\nWhy the world is after US?<br />\n<br />\nThe secret lies in the American spending, that they hardly save. In fact they use their credit cards to spend their future income. That the US spends &nbsp;is what makes it attractive to export to the US . So US imports more than what it exports year after year.<br />\n<br />\nThe result:<br />\n<br />\nThe world is dependent on US consumption for its growth. By its deepening culture of consumption, the US has habituated the world to feed on US consumption. But as the US needs money to finance its consumption, the world provides the money.<br />\n<br />\nIt's like a shopkeeper providing the money to a customer so that the customer keeps buying from the shop. If the customer will not buy, the shop won't have business, unless the shopkeeper funds him. The US is like the lucky customer. And the world is like the helpless shopkeeper financier.<br />\n<br />\nWho is America 's biggest shopkeeper financier? Japan of course. Yet it's Japan which is regarded as weak. Modern economists complain that Japanese do not spend, so they do not grow. To force the Japanese to spend, the Japanese &nbsp;government exerted itself, reduced the savings rates, even charged the savers. Even then the Japanese did not spend (habits don't change, even with taxes, do they?). Their traditional postal savings alone is over $1.2 trillion, about three times the Indian GDP. Thus, savings, far from being the strength of Japan , has become its pain.<br />\n<br />\nHence, what is the lesson?<br />\n<br />\nThat is, a nation cannot grow unless the people spend, not save. Not just spend, but borrow and spend. Dr. Jagdish Bhagwati, the famous Indian-born economist in the US , told Manmohan Singh that Indians wastefully save. Ask them to spend, on imported cars and, seriously, even on cosmetics! This will put India on a growth curve. This is one of the reason for MNC's coming down to India , seeing the consumer spending.<br />\n<br />\n'Saving is sin, and spending is virtue.'<br />\n<br />\nBut before you follow this Neo Economics, get some fools to &nbsp;save so that you can borrow from them and spend !!!</span><br />\n<br />\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">We all know that <span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">inflation is caused by money supply growing faster than the rate of economic growth</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">.&nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">The task of keeping the rate of inflation low and stable is usually given to</span></span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">the</span></span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;central banks</span></span><span class=\"apple-converted-space\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">&nbsp;</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">that control the size of the money supply through the setting of interest rates</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">, through open market operations</span></span><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">, and through the setting of banking reserve requirements.</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">HOW DOES THE CORRUPT US FEDERAL RESERVE SYSTEM WORK? <o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is real\u2014and NOT an imaginary story like the traveller in Alabama. &nbsp;</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">How does the US monetary system work ?</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is bound to shock you out of your skin.<o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4kbPsNGI/AAAAAAAAC3Y/1YOKEpiQUyE/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4kbPsNGI/AAAAAAAAC3Y/1YOKEpiQUyE/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><span class=\"apple-style-span\"><span style=\"line-height: 115%;\">Pass on this expose\u2014for unless you understand , you cannot be free</span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 14px;\">.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4gU922aI/AAAAAAAAC3U/FYC22U_SxIA/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4gU922aI/AAAAAAAAC3U/FYC22U_SxIA/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"line-height: 14px;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Taking on nearly religious proportions, the established monetary institution exists as one of the most unquestioned forms of faith there is. How money is created, the policies by which it is governed and how it truly affects society are unregistered interests of the great majority of the population.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">In a world where 1% of the population owns 40% of the planet\u2019s wealth\u2026in a world where 34,000 children die every single day from poverty and preventable diseases, and where 50% of the world\u2019s population lives on less than 2 dollars a day\u2026 one thing is clear:</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Something is terribly wrong.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">And whether we are aware of it or not, the lifeblood of all of our established institutions and thus society itself, is money. Therefore understanding this institution of monetary policy is critical to understanding why our lives are the way they are.<br />\n<br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Unfortunately, economics is often viewed with confusion and boredom. Endless streams of financial jargon coupled with intimidating mathematics quickly deter people from attempts at understanding it. However, the fact is, the complexity associated with the financial system is a mere mask, designed to conceal one of the most socially paralyzing structures humanity has ever endured.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;\"None are more hopelessly enslaved than those who falsely believe they are free.\"-Johann Wolfgang von Goethe<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The United States Government decides it needs some money, so it calls up the Federal Reserve, and requests, say, 10 billion dollars\u201d. The fed replies, saying \u201d sure\u2026 we\u2019ll buy 10 billion in government bonds from you.\u201d</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4YmmuOLI/AAAAAAAAC3M/iH8rcsVLCxI/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4YmmuOLI/AAAAAAAAC3M/iH8rcsVLCxI/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nSo, the government then takes some piece of paper, paints some official looking designs on them, and calls them \u2018Treasury Bonds\u2019. Then, it puts a value on these Bonds to the sum of 10 billion dollars, and sends them over to the Fed. In turn, the people at the Fed draw up a bunch of impressive pieces of paper themselves, only this time calling them \u2018Federal Reserve Notes\u2019\u2026also designating a value of 10 billion dollars to the set.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4V505ElI/AAAAAAAAC3I/HFWVcFW-76o/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO4V505ElI/AAAAAAAAC3I/HFWVcFW-76o/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nThe Fed then takes these notes and trades them for the Bonds. Once this exchange is complete, the government then takes the 10 billion in Federal Reserve Notes and deposits it into a bank account\u2026and upon this deposit, the paper notes officially become \u2018legal tender\u2019 money, adding 10 billion to the US money supply. And there it is\u2026 10 billion in new money has been created.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n</div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO5uBsp5II/AAAAAAAAC3o/tpWmEbO43pM/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO5uBsp5II/AAAAAAAAC3o/tpWmEbO43pM/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Of course, this example is a generalization, for, in reality, this transaction would occur electronically, with no paper used at all. In fact only 3% of the US money supply exists in physical currency. The other 97% essentially exists in computers alone.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO5BumIG0I/AAAAAAAAC3g/RZZcykDTn6c/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO5BumIG0I/AAAAAAAAC3g/RZZcykDTn6c/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Now, Government bonds are, by design, instruments of Debt and when the Fed purchases these bonds, with money it created essentially out of thin air, the government is actually promising to pay back that money to the Fed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">In other words\u2026 The money was created out of debt. This mind numbing paradox of how money, or value, can be created out of debt, or a liability, will become more clear as we further this exercise.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">So, the exchange has been made and now 10 billion dollars sits in a commercial bank account. Here is where it gets really interesting, for as based on the Fractional Reserve practice, that 10 billion dollar deposit instantly becomes part of the bank\u2019s Reserves, just as all deposits do. And regarding reserve requirements, as stated in Modern money mechanics:</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nA bank must maintain legally required reserves, equal to a prescribed percentage of its deposits. It then quantifies this by stating: under current regulations, the reserve requirement against most transaction accounts is 10%.\u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">This means that with a ten billion dollar deposit, 10% or 1 billion is held as the required reserve, while the other 9 billion is considered an excessive reserve and can be used as the basis for new loans.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nNow, it is logical to assume that this 9 billion is literally coming out of the existing 10 billion dollars deposit. However, this is actually not the case. What really happens is that the 9 billion is simply created out of thin air, on top of the existing 10 billion dollar deposit. This is how the money supply is expanded.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The banks do not really pay out loans from the money they receive as deposits. If they did this, no additional money would be created. What they do when they make loans is to accept promissory notes (loan contracts) in exchange for credits (money) to the borrower\u2019s transaction accounts.\u201d</span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO6Gm6KafI/AAAAAAAAC3s/Lz7lqhGEl2I/s1600/download+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO6Gm6KafI/AAAAAAAAC3s/Lz7lqhGEl2I/s1600/download+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nIn other words, the 9 billion can be created out of nothing, simply because there is a demand for such a loan, and there is a 10 billion dollars deposit to satisfy the reserve requirements.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nNow, let\u2019s assume that somebody walks into this bank and borrows the available 9 billion dollars. They will then most likely take that money and deposit it into their own bank account.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <br />\nThe process then repeats, for that deposit becomes part of the banks reserves, 10% is isolated and in turn 90% of the 9 billion or 8.1 billion is now available as newly created money for more loans. And, of course, that 8.1 can be loaned out and redeposited creating an additional 7.2 billion\u2026to 6.5 billion.. to 5.9 billion etc.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nThis deposit-money creation-loan cycle can technically go on to infinity\u2026 the average mathematical result is that about 90 billion dollars can be created on top of the original 10 billion. In other words, for every deposit that ever occurs in the banking system, about 9 times that amount can be created out of thin air.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">So that we understand how money is created by this fractional reserve banking system ,a</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;logical, yet elusive question might come to mind:</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nWhat is actually giving this newly created money value?</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nThe answer: The money that already exists.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The new money essentially steals value from the existing money supply\u2026 for the total pool of money is being increased, irrespective to demand for goods and services, and, as supply and demand finds equilibrium- prices rise, diminishing the purchasing power of each individual dollar.&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">T<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">his is generally referred to as \u2018inflation\u2019 and inflation is essentially a hidden tax on the public</span>. ( I thing we have given Manmohan Singh and Montek Singh Ahluwalia enough time to figure out all this !)</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">What is the advice that you generally get, and that is inflate the currency. They don`t say debase the currency, they don`t say devalue the currency, they don`t say cheat the people with savings, they say lower the interest rates.</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPxR-TwTCI/AAAAAAAAC6s/l3OvmY78jWM/s1600/images+%252852%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPxR-TwTCI/AAAAAAAAC6s/l3OvmY78jWM/s1600/images+%252852%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPxZW9OsJI/AAAAAAAAC6w/RbWN8xwyrFg/s1600/images+%252853%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPxZW9OsJI/AAAAAAAAC6w/RbWN8xwyrFg/s1600/images+%252853%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The real deception is when we distort the value of money, when we create money out of thin air, we have no savings yet there`s so called capitol\u2026so the question boils down to this-how in the world can we expect to solve the problems of inflation\u2013that is the increase in the supply of money\u2013 with more inflation? \u201d<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Of course, it can\u2019t. The Fractional Reserve System of monetary expansion is inherently.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\ninflationary. For the act of expanding the money supply without there being a proportional expand of good and services in the economy, will always debase a currency..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">In fact a quick glance at the historical values of the US dollars Vs the money supply,r</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">eflects this point definitively, for the inverse relationship is obvious.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nIn fact, One dollar in 1913 required 21.60 cents in 2007, to match value\u2026that is a 96% devaluation since the Federal reserve has come into existence.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPwwDujJ0I/AAAAAAAAC6o/lH7Ir3y7Rrk/s1600/images+%252851%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPwwDujJ0I/AAAAAAAAC6o/lH7Ir3y7Rrk/s1600/images+%252851%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Now, if this realty of inherent and perpetual inflation seems absurd and economically&nbsp;self-defeating\u2026 hold that thought, for absurdity is an understatement in regard to how our financial system really operates.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">For in US financial system money is debt and debt is money.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">-- the more money there is, the more debt there is\u2026 the more debt there is, the more money there is.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPv-KUl8aI/AAAAAAAAC6c/ojulITpDVCg/s1600/images+%252848%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPv-KUl8aI/AAAAAAAAC6c/ojulITpDVCg/s1600/images+%252848%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPwIWLBzuI/AAAAAAAAC6g/D6C_XEj-1B4/s1600/images+%252849%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPwIWLBzuI/AAAAAAAAC6g/D6C_XEj-1B4/s1600/images+%252849%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">To put it a different way, every single dollar in your wallet is owed to somebody by somebody; for remember, the only way the money can come into existence is from loans. Therefore, if everyone in the country were able to pay off all debts, including the government, there would not be one dollar in circulation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">(If there were no debts in US money system, there wouldn`t be any money\u201d<br />\n<br />\n<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">The international bankers installed a central bank in 1913\u2026The Federal Reserve. And as long as this institution exists, perpetual debt is guaranteed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Now, so far we have discussed the reality that money is created out of debt, through loans.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPwWoSx_-I/AAAAAAAAC6k/x8gngSgYae4/s1600/images+%252850%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPwWoSx_-I/AAAAAAAAC6k/x8gngSgYae4/s1600/images+%252850%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <br />\nThese loans are based on a bank\u2019s \u201cReserves\u201d and Reserves are derived from deposits. Through this fractional reserve system, any one deposit can create 9 times its original value, in turn debasing the existing money supply, raising prices in society.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPvttIO9RI/AAAAAAAAC6Y/5d0wldcCQFw/s1600/images+%252847%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPvttIO9RI/AAAAAAAAC6Y/5d0wldcCQFw/s1600/images+%252847%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <br />\nAnd since all this money is created out of debt and circulated randomly through commerce, people become detached from their original debt and a disequilibrium exists where people are forced to compete for labor, in order to pull enough money out of the money supply to cover their costs of living.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">As dysfunctional and backwards as all of this might seem\u2026 there is still one thing we have omitted from this equation\u2026 and it is this element of the structure which reveals the truly fraudulent nature of the system itself.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n-The application of Interest.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nWhen the government borrows money from the Fed or when person borrows money from a bank, it almost always has to be paid back with accrued interest. In other words, almost every single dollar that exists must be eventually returned to a bank, with interest paid as well.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPvZzK8xlI/AAAAAAAAC6U/S3HTFqK8coQ/s1600/images+%252846%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"153\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPvZzK8xlI/AAAAAAAAC6U/S3HTFqK8coQ/s320/images+%252846%2529.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">But, if all money is borrowed from the central bank and is expanded by the commercial banks through loans, only what would be referred to as the \u2018principle\u2019 is being created in the money supply\u2026. So then, where is the money to cover all of the interest that is charged?</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nNowhere. It doesn\u2019t exist. The ramifications of this are staggering, for the amount of money owed back to the banks will always exceed the amount of money that is available in circulation. This is why Inflation is a constant in the economy, for new money is always needed to help cover the perpetual deficit built into the system, caused by the&nbsp;the need to pay the interest.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">What this also means is that mathematically, defaults and bankruptcy are literally built into the system. And there will always be poor pockets of society that get the short end of the stick. An analogy would be a game of musical chairs, for once the music stops someone is left out to dry.</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nAnd that\u2019s the point. It invariably transfers true wealth from the individual to the banks, for if you are unable to pay for your mortgage, they will take your property.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPuKRiEH2I/AAAAAAAAC6I/dCU4oMw0978/s1600/images+%252843%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPuKRiEH2I/AAAAAAAAC6I/dCU4oMw0978/s1600/images+%252843%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">This is particularly enraging when you realize that not only is such a default inevitable due to the fractional reserve practice, but also because of the fact that the money that the bank loaned to you didn\u2019t even legally exist in the first place.<o:p></o:p></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTP1uHZAF9I/AAAAAAAAC68/oIetDJ9BFRY/s1600/images+%252856%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTP1uHZAF9I/AAAAAAAAC68/oIetDJ9BFRY/s1600/images+%252856%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>In the 1969, there was a Minnesota court case involving a man named Jerome Daly, who was challenging the foreclosure of his home by the bank, which provided the loan to purchase it. His argument was that the mortgage contract required both parties, being he and the bank, each put up a legitimate form of property for the exchange. In legal language, this is called \u201cconsideration\u201d.<o:p></o:p></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPuusZ1vcI/AAAAAAAAC6Q/cUa3tSzxZJY/s1600/images+%252845%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPuusZ1vcI/AAAAAAAAC6Q/cUa3tSzxZJY/s1600/images+%252845%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>(Consideration: -a contract`s basis. A contract is founded on an exchange of one form of consideration for another.)<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Mr. Daly explained that the money was, in fact, not the property of the bank, for it was created out of nothing as soon as the loan agreement was signed.</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPudMwGrOI/AAAAAAAAC6M/Nwj5dU_L2JM/s1600/images+%252844%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPudMwGrOI/AAAAAAAAC6M/Nwj5dU_L2JM/s1600/images+%252844%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <br />\nRemember what modern money mechanics stated about loans: \u201cwhat they do when they make loans is to accept promissory notes in exchange for credits\u2026Reserves are unchanged by the loan transactions. But deposit credits constitute new additions to the total deposits of the banking system.\u201d In other words, the money doesn\u2019t come out of any of their existing assets. The bank is simply inventing it, putting up nothing of its own except for a theoretical liability on paper.<o:p></o:p></i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO80jYLegI/AAAAAAAAC4o/LHvcBDWE36w/s1600/images+%252821%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO80jYLegI/AAAAAAAAC4o/LHvcBDWE36w/s1600/images+%252821%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>As the court case progressed, the banks president, Mr. Morgan, took the stand, and in the judge\u2019s personal memorandum, he recalled that \u201cThe Plaintiff (bank\u2019s president) admitted that it, in combination with the Federal Reserve Bank\u2026did create the\u2026money and credit upon its books by bookkeeping entry\u2026the money and credit first came into existence when they created it\u2026Mr. Morgan admitted that no United States law or statute existed which gave him the right to do this\u2026a lawful consideration must exist and be tendered to support the note.\u201d \u201cThe jury found that there was no lawful consideration and I agree\u201d He also poetically added, \u201d Only God can create something of value out of nothing\u201d<o:p></o:p></i></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO9Il4vWWI/AAAAAAAAC4s/NiOJe1DanOo/s1600/download+%25284%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTO9Il4vWWI/AAAAAAAAC4s/NiOJe1DanOo/s1600/download+%25284%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>And upon that revelation, the court rejected the bank\u2019s claim for foreclosure and Daly kept his home. The implications of this court decision are immense, for every time you borrow money from a bank, whether it is a mortgage loan or a credit card charge, the money given to you is not only counterfeit, it is an illegitimate form of consideration and hence voids the contract to repay\u2026 for the bank never had the money as property to begin with. Unfortunately, such legal realizations are suppressed and ignored, and the game of perpetual wealth transfer and perpetual debt continues\u2026.</i></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nAnd this brings us to the ultimate question: why?<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">During the American civil war president Lincoln bypassed the high-interest loans offered by the European banks and decided to do what the founding fathers advocated, which was to create an independent and inherently debt-free currency. It was called the Greenback. Shortly after this measure was taken, an internal document circulated between private British and American banking interests stated:</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPteTLuuJI/AAAAAAAAC6A/k1YMl9CF3QI/s1600/images+%252841%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPteTLuuJI/AAAAAAAAC6A/k1YMl9CF3QI/s1600/images+%252841%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; <br />\n\u201c\u2026slavery is but the owning of labor and carries with it the care of laborers, while the European plan\u2026is that capital shall control labor by controlling wages.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">This can be done by controlling the money. It will not do to allow the greenback, as we cannot control that.\u201d-The Hazard Circular, July, 1862</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPnIjoMuxI/AAAAAAAAC5M/dBclfMWjTtM/s1600/images+%252829%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPnIjoMuxI/AAAAAAAAC5M/dBclfMWjTtM/s1600/images+%252829%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\nThe fractional reserve policy perpetrated by the Federal Reserve, which has spread in practice to the great majority of banks in the world is, in fact, a system of modern slavery. Think about it\u2026&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPtv_ulrKI/AAAAAAAAC6E/c4kKVtCQepA/s1600/images+%252842%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPtv_ulrKI/AAAAAAAAC6E/c4kKVtCQepA/s1600/images+%252842%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">Money is created out of debt. They submit to employment to pay it off.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPtNLLJICI/AAAAAAAAC58/uL-NkASD9Do/s1600/images+%252840%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPtNLLJICI/AAAAAAAAC58/uL-NkASD9Do/s1600/images+%252840%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">But, if money can only be created out of loans, how can society ever be debt free? It can\u2019t. And that\u2019s the point.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp; </span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">And it is the fear of losing assets, coupled with the struggle to keep up with the perpetual debt and inflation inherent in the system, compounded by the inescapable scarcity within the money supply itself created by the interest that can never be repaid\u2026 that keeps the wage slave in line\u2026 running on the hamster wheel with the millions of others\u2026 in effect powering an Empire that truly benefits only the elite at the top of the pyramid\u2026&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPsaCzvvwI/AAAAAAAAC54/BT2Z_xzutEw/s1600/images+%252839%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTPsaCzvvwI/AAAAAAAAC54/BT2Z_xzutEw/s1600/images+%252839%2529.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp;&nbsp;</span></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 16.8pt; margin: 0in 0in 7.5pt;\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">---for at the end of day, who are you really working for? Therefore people cannot be fair and people do not trust each other.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">A guy will come over to you and say, \u201cI\u2019ve got just the house you\u2019re looking for\u201d.&nbsp;</span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">He\u2019s a salesman.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">When a doctor says \u2018I think your kidney has to come out\u2019, I don\u2019t know if he\u2019s trying to pay off a yacht, or that my kidney has to come out- it\u2019s hard in monetary system to trust people.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\"><br />\n</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\">\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;arial&quot; , &quot;helvetica&quot; , sans-serif;\">If a company dumps toxic waste into the ocean to save money, most people recognize this as corrupt behavior. The paper reached a circulation of 900,000 by 1925, second only to the New York Daily News run from the shadows by Jew Rothschild.<br /><br />Henry Ford knew that Jew Rothschild would start world wars to carve out the state of Israel and to make money out of war. Ford wrote that parasite Jews, in their role as financiers, contributed nothing of value to society.<br /><br />Ford once bit into a candy bar and, finding it not as good as it once had been, said \"The Jews have taken hold of it. They've cheapened it to make more money\".<br /><br />In 1915 Ford blamed Jews for instigating World War I, saying \"I know who caused the war: German-Jewish bankers.\"<br /><br />In 1925, Ford said \"What I oppose most is the international Jewish money power that is met in every war. That is what I oppose \u2013 a power that has no country and that can order the young men of all countries out to death.\"<br /><br />One of the articles, \"Jewish Power and America's Money Famine\", asserted that the power exercised by Jews over the nation's supply of money was insidious, depriving farmers and others outside the banking coterie of money when they needed it most. The article asked the question: \"Where is the American gold supply? ... It may be in the United States but it does not belong to the United States.\" It concluded that Jews controlled the gold supply and, hence, American money<br />Another article, \"Jewish Idea Molded Federal Reserve System\", was a reflection of Ford's distrust of the Federal Reserve System and its proponent, Paul Warburg. Ford believed the Federal Reserve system was secretive and insidious<br /><br />Many issues of the Independent comment extensively upon The Protocols of the Elders of Zion. The first mention of the Protocols appears in the issue of July 10, 1920, the seventh installment of its \"International Jew\" series.<br /><br />Also, in 1920\u201321 the Independent carried a series of articles expanding on the themes of financial control by Jews, entitled:-----<br /><br />Jewish Idea in American Monetary Affairs: The remarkable story of Paul Warburg, who began work on the United States monetary system after three weeks residence in this country<br />Jewish Idea Molded Federal Reserve System: What Baruch was in War Material, Paul Warburg was in War Finances; Some Curious revelations of money and politics.<br />Jewish Idea of a Central Bank for America: The evolution of Paul M. Warburg's idea of Federal Reserve System without government management.<br />How Jewish International Finance Functions: The Warburg family and firm divided the world between them and did amazing things which non-Jews could not do<br />Jewish Power and America's Money Famine: The Warburg Federal Reserve sucks money to New York, leaving productive sections of the country in disastrous need.<br />The Economic Plan of International Jews: An outline of the Protocolists' monetary policy, with notes on the parallel found in Jewish financial practice.<br /><br /><span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/01/murky-truths-of-inflation-and.html<br /><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.in/2011/02/worth-more-than-sum-total-of-entire.html</span><br /><br />The ADL mobilized prominent Jews to publicly oppose Ford's message. They formed a coalition of Jewish groups for the same purpose and raised constant objections in the Detroit press. text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTKuLu_47MI/AAAAAAAAC2Q/sq9RgezOyCM/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTKuLu_47MI/AAAAAAAAC2Q/sq9RgezOyCM/s1600/images+%252818%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nThe Engine staff was good enough to carry on with telephonic guidance--so i gave orders to the steward to feed him in bed. --and also to replace his soft matress with a hard one .<br />\n<br />\n( now, i cant do this as per regulations, and can lose my own job and be disgraced , if my company knows about this . Captain is not expected to run his chemical tanker on sentiments, as lives could be lost . But then this is the meaning of compassion )<br />\n<br />\nLater I went to visit him and he was praying while lying down with rosary in one hand and the picture of Jesus in the other--looking very distraught.<br />\n<br />\nI asked him \" Tell me exactly how you hurt your back, this bad!\"<br />\n<br />\nHe said \" Half the men in cold countries have the same problem, caused due to shovelling heavy snow\"<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHuUZTxgeI/AAAAAAAAC1E/bF38rRxyVmk/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHuUZTxgeI/AAAAAAAAC1E/bF38rRxyVmk/s1600/images+%25282%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nThen he showed me a picture of himself shovelling snow at his porch.<br />\n<br />\nTo be frank i found the shovel of STUPID ergometric design. Naturally he had hurt his lower back.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHunQlX-JI/AAAAAAAAC1M/0ru-fk7nkpA/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHunQlX-JI/AAAAAAAAC1M/0ru-fk7nkpA/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nAs you grow older your back muscles get stiff in cold and and can cause both muscular and disc injuries.<br />\n<br />\n<br />\nSo i gave him a few shovelling tips, where the principle of PREVENTION was paramount --<br />\n<br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">1) Change your stupid shovel and use a ergonomic hoe type spade</span> .</i><br />\n<i><br />\n</i><br />\n<i>2) <span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: red;\">Never ever bend your back, stand upright. If you have to lower yourself use the thigh muscles.</span></i><br />\n<i><br />\n</i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">3) Don't do repetitive action, &nbsp;continuously.</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><br />\n</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\">4) Wear a back support while doing the job</span></i><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTKuAe80c5I/AAAAAAAAC2I/rqxhgTq8fmw/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTKuAe80c5I/AAAAAAAAC2I/rqxhgTq8fmw/s1600/images+%252810%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nAfter the next winter , I got a call from him. Thanks! Your advise worked!!<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTKuFTGuKqI/AAAAAAAAC2M/dbOLjr-B6pc/s1600/download.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTKuFTGuKqI/AAAAAAAAC2M/dbOLjr-B6pc/s1600/download.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nSo read this with an open mind. It may work for you too.<br />\n<br />\nThe hoe type spade must be in two sizes--one large and one small.<br />\n<br />\nThe smaller hoe must have a longer handle.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHuxyaS8TI/AAAAAAAAC1Q/-3GjNkcmH5Q/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHuxyaS8TI/AAAAAAAAC1Q/-3GjNkcmH5Q/s1600/images+%25285%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nIn India nobody ever uses a spade, which hurts the lower back.<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHu-IIY8nI/AAAAAAAAC1U/wzBLJ7rotJI/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHu-IIY8nI/AAAAAAAAC1U/wzBLJ7rotJI/s1600/images+%25283%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nChop, lever up , shorten the handle , throw-- all the time standing upright. &nbsp;Do not scoop up too much wet snow.<br />\n<br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow; font-size: large;\">Ice-denizens , pl pass this around</span> --<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHvF6IdAKI/AAAAAAAAC1Y/y97_HiseKAk/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHvF6IdAKI/AAAAAAAAC1Y/y97_HiseKAk/s1600/images+%25288%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nCHANGE IS THE ONLY CONSTANT IN LIFE.<br />\n<br />\nOn our ships , our rat guards have been falling off for the past 500 years , and will continue to do so for the next 500 years. On all the thousands of ships all over the world!<br />\n<br />\nMy son at Cornell, when he was 8 years old , sailed with me.<br />\n<br />\nOne day he asked me \" Daddy, why are sailors so stupid. &nbsp;All ships keep replacing their rat guards on the mooring ropes, which fall off every half an hour. Why don't you sailors put the hole off-centre, so that the centre of gravity of the metal sheet shifts downwards and gravity will keep the rat guard in place\" ?<br />\n<br />\nThis coloured picture is just to imagine-- how to shift the centre of gravity, downwards !-- it is moronic to hang weights!!<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHyOfB7gxI/AAAAAAAAC18/xlMB8K-wT6c/s1600/images.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHyOfB7gxI/AAAAAAAAC18/xlMB8K-wT6c/s1600/images.jpg\" /></a></div><br />\nThis is the usual stupid rat guard with a hole in the exact centre-- one tiny gust of wind and it falls off.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHxsIq1MBI/AAAAAAAAC1w/Q7wr0FQotgg/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTHxsIq1MBI/AAAAAAAAC1w/Q7wr0FQotgg/s1600/images+%25281%2529.jpg\" /></a></div><div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\"><br />\n</div>&nbsp;Yes- at sea we too suffer from a severe lack of brains!--like the snow shovellers!!<br />\n<div><br />\nIf you cant get the hardware, just improvise-- see video below-- so that you<span style=\"color: red; Conditions<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New the pre-layer causing a<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i>reddish brown discoloration. If the toluene or xylene concentrations are<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i>too high the entire pre-layer up to the indicating layer is discoloured making<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i>a benzene measurement impossible. Petroleum hydrocarbons, alcohols<o:p></o:p></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i>and esters do not affect the indication.</i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-size: 8.5pt;\"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i><br />\n</i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal;
