margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-style: normal; line-height: 24px;\"><b>Example of a Draeger Phenol tube instruction sheet:--</b></span></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: normal; margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><span style=\"color: black;\"><i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-style: normal; line-height: 24px;\"><br />\n</span></i></span></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i></i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Phenol Application Range</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Standard Measuring Range: 1 to 20 ppm</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Number of Strokes n: 20</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Time for Measurement: app. 5 min</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Standard Deviation: \u00b1 10 to 15 %</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Colour Change: yellow \u2014&gt; brown grey</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Ambient Operating Conditions</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Temperature: 10 to 30 \u00b0C</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Absolute Humidity: 1 to 18 mg H2O / L</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Reaction Principle</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>C6H5OH + Ce(SO4)2 + H2SO4 \u2014&gt; brown grey reaction product</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Cross Sensivity</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Cresols are alse indicated, but with different sensitivities. To determine</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>m-cresol multiply the indication by 0.8.</i></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"margin-bottom: 0.0001pt;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif;\"><i>Benzene, I noticed a American serial \" The Simpsons\" , occupied a lot of MB space, and decided to delete it.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">Suddenly i realised that my elder son , would not save a TV serial unless it was worth it.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">At random i selected a video clip and put it on play , in the middle of the episode.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">What i saw made me have the heartiest laugh of the decade.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">To save the town from pollution someone was covering up the town with a huge glass bubble. Suddenly the drunks in a tavern and rabid \"praise the lord party\" in a church felt that apocalypse is comin' -- that the sky is about to fall and they would die.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">Suddenly two groups started running out-- one from the church and the other from the tavern. The hilarious part is the entire drunken party ran to the church to pray fervently , and the entire pious party ran to the bar to get drunk--passing each other on the way , ignoring each other !</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">This got me interested , and i am glad i saw the series.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">The creator Matt Groening is a genius. Whether any Yank agrees with me or not, i would say he is one of &nbsp;the greatest living geniuses .&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">The serial is a satirical parody of the quintessential all American family. It lampoons the dysfunctional family along with yank culture and society in a tongue in cheek way, which keeps you in splits.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">Most of the time you have to read between the lines. So a moron or a duffer may ask \" what is the big deal? \" . &nbsp;Let them have their own super buffoon Mr.Bean.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">The Simpsons full length movie is one of the highest grossers.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">The Brits who love this longest running American serial of 20 years , has put a catch exclamation \" DOH! \" ( means you are pissed off ) in their dictionary.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">I wish they would include:--</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">\"magumba\" ( large breasts ) too , which makes jogging a spectator sport.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">other pearls: --</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">\"<i>pull a homer</i> \"-- ( to succeed despite being an idiot )</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">\"<i>spiritual de-pantsing</i> \" --( Karmic fall from grace )</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\">\"<i>texas penny\"</i>&nbsp;---( hundred dollar bill )</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\"><span style=\"font-family: Times, 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: large; line-height: 115%;\">Homer, the obese dad, works as a safety inspector at the Springfield Nuclear Power Plant, a position at odds with his careless, buffoonish personality. He is married to Marge Simpson, a stereotypical American housewife and mother. They have three children: Bart, a ten-year-old troublemaker; Lisa, a precocious eight-year-old activist; and Maggie, the baby of the family who rarely speaks, but communicates by sucking on a pacifier. HE SHOULD STICK TO TAMIL PRIDE AGAMA SHIT.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">I DARE ANY WOMAN WHOSE KNOWN PERIODS ARE ONE WEEK AWAY.. CLIMB SABARIMALA AND YOUR MENSTRUAL BLOOD WILL FLOW OUT BETWEEN YOUR LEGS..</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">THE WOMAN WHO CONCEIVES AFTER THIS FAILED MENSTRUAL CYCLE GETS STILL BORN BABIES ..</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The endometrium is the tissue lining the uterus (or womb). The endometrium is soft and spongy. Each month, the endometrium changes as part of the menstrual cycle.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Early in the cycle, the ovaries secrete a hormone called estrogen that causes the endometrium to thicken. In the middle of the cycle, the ovaries start secreting another hormone called progesterone. Progesterone prepares the innermost layer of the endometrium to support an embryo should conception (pregnancy) occur.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">If conception does not occur, the hormone levels decrease dramatically. The innermost layer of the endometrium is then shed as menstrual fluid. This leads to the cyclical nature of the menstrual cycle.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Because the endometrium builds up between menstrual cycles and then sheds during menstruation, the endometrium is thickest just before menstruation&nbsp;</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">One of the functions of progesterone is to oppose estrogen, which causes the uterus to shed the endometrium during menstruation before a new cycle of proliferation, or building up, begins in preparation for the next menstruation.</span></div>\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: medium;\">POSITIVE SCALAR ENERGY CAUSES THE ENDOMETRIUM SLOUGHING OFF TO BE INCOMPLETE..</span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Endometriosis occurs when the uterine tissue implants and grows outside of the uterus \u2014 often affecting the function of the ovaries, uterus and fallopian tubes.</span><br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">If the endometrium travels outside the fallopian tube and to the other areas of the body, it results in endometriosis. The hormones produced during the menstrual cycle will stimulate this extra tissue to grow, break down and bleed in the uterus.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: medium;\">The shredded tissue and blood have nowhere to exit the body and can develop into cysts, adhesions and scar tissues over time rendering a woman PERMANENTLY INFERTILE.</span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Retrograde menstrual flow, where some of the menstrual tissue flows back into the abdomen and gets implanted there. In endometriosis, the abnormal cells or scar tissues block the ovaries and fallopian tube.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: purple; font-size: medium;\">An egg usually travels from the ovary, along the fallopian tube, and into the uterus for fertilization before implantation. If you have endometriosis in the fallopian tube, the tissue will block the egg from passing into the uterus.</span></div>\n<span style=\"color: purple; font-size: medium;\"></span><br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: purple; Parashurama created Kerala by throwing his axe into the Arabian sea , as per legend.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He was the Guru of several Indian stalwarts like Drona and Bhishma of Mahabharat , and for Karna , Lord Ayyappa, the diety of Sabarimala and Lord Rama, <span style=\"color: red;\">&nbsp;in a \"one way direction\"</span>.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Parashurama was upset with Sri Ram for breaking his Shiva's bow, which he had given to King Janaka for safe keeping. So when Ram was on the way back to Ayodhya with his new bride Sita and Lakshman he accosted him, and gave him the bow of Vishnu to string.( Ram recognised Parashurama but Parashurama did NOT know the \"real\" Ram ) .&nbsp;</i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br /></i></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>Ram strung Vishnu's bow easily, and pointed the arrow at Parashurama. &nbsp;Parashurama suddenly felt all his martial and spiritual energy drained out out his body -- and he suddenly realised that Ram is Vishnu avatar himself. &nbsp;Ram then shot the arrow ( missile ) into the sky, after uttering the trigger mantra . &nbsp;</i></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i><br /></i></span>\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><i>After that Parashurama went for sanyas to Mahendra Parvat and was never ever seen -- Parashurama he is a iccha mrithyu Vishnu avatar . Parashurama will be the MARTIAL GURU of Vishnu's 10th avatar Kalki.</i></span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It was Parashurama who installed the Ayurveda god Dhanwantari idols in Kerala.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It is on this day 6000 years ago that the great Bheeshma of Mahabharata decides to leave his body behind on a bed of arrows and ascend to heaven, in the presence of Lord Krishna and Arjun--exactly as per the Iccha Mrityu &nbsp;( death at will ) boon given by his father.&nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; Knowing this, immediately after the coronation, Yudhisthira, accompanied by Lord Krishna and his brothers, went to Bheeshma. Before leaving his mortal body, Bheeshma gives a long discourse to Yudhisthira on various aspects of life and Dharma. After listening to everything, Yudhisthira wants to know if there is any one thing through which one can achieve all; and Bheeshma prescribes the Viashnusahasranama stotra. The first 13 stanzas are the dialog between Yudhisthira and Bheeshma.</span></span></i><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;serif&quot;; Getting angry the short fused Parashurama attacked the noble Bheeshma, who was equally good in fighting .&nbsp;</span></i><br />\n<i><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">This is a holy ritual fire, lit at a specific time, on a hill east of the sannidhanam &nbsp; -- NOT a celestial star, which has to do with precession. &nbsp;</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Lit three times to represent Tamas/ Rajas/ Sattva--the trident of Lord Shiva. This is a signal for the pilgrims to chant SWAMIYEE-- SHARANAMAYYAPPA</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Pilgrims have to cleanse themselves with 41 days of fasting , prayer and abstain from worldy pleasures , before they take the dangerous trek through dark jungles infested with tigers, with bare feet.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">A large posse of policemen do crowd control .</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/_tugjD0mUn6M/TTQftzer7KI/AAAAAAAAC7o/GUsjiK63BuY/s1600/sabarimalai_20406f.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Let me talk about of Kerala hero and founder --Lord Parashurama. He was the great grandson of Brigu Rishi, who lived on the banks of river Saraswati in 4400 BC.. He was the youngest of the 5 children of Jamagdhani and Renuka, and was a gifted wielder of weapons.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">One day King Sahsrarjuna killed his father. Seeing his mother terribly distraught he swore to take revenge and also kill every Kshtriya of the clan.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">First he killed all the sons of Sahasarjuna with his battle axe and then he went around in a mad frenzy , killing every Kshatriya he came across, till his grandfather Richeek Rishi stopped him.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He did the Ashwemedha sacrifice , which only Kings are allowed to do , disregarding protocol, and then came to Kerala, where he donated land to the Namboodiris. </span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Parshurama was the great Guru of Dronacharya , the Guru of the Pandavas and Kauravas .</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The Sabarimala pilgrimage is about COLLECTIVE QUANTUM CONSCIOUSNESS , where millions of people with one single intent , chant the mantra \"<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"color: blue;\"><i> swamiyee sharanamayyapa</i></span> \" in unison while watching a single bright object the Makara Vilakku. &nbsp;( 51 million pilgrims visited the temple in 2010-- this is the population of some large countries on this planet).</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The atmosphere there at this time is electric , and the frenzy has to be seen and felt to be believed-- where even your body hairs stand up.</span><br />\n<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; A WIDOWER OR A BACHELOR CANNOT PERFORM A YAGNA..</span></div>\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">Marriage ( vivaha ) is known as \"saha-dharma-carini-samprayoga\". It means \"union with a wife together with whom a man practises dharma\".</span><span style=\"color: blue; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">&nbsp;</span></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"></span><br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The clear implication is that carnal pleasure is not its chief purpose, but the pursuit of dharma.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\"><br /></span></div>\n<span style=\"color: blue; font-size: large;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">The sastras do not ask a man to pursue dharma all by himself but require him to take a helpmate for it. The wife is called \"dharma-patni\", \"saha-dharma-carini\", thus underlining her connection with dharma, and not with sensual pleasure.&nbsp;</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\">Here is proof of the high esteem in which the sastras hold women.</span><br />\n<br />\n<div>\n<span style=\"color: purple; font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif; font-size: large;\">THE INDIAN JUDICIARY WITH BENAMI MEDIA AND NCW IN CAHOOTS HAS REDUCED AN INDIAN WOMAN TO A SEX OBJECT..</span></div>\n<br />\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;times new roman&quot; , &quot;times&quot; , &quot;freeserif&quot; , serif;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/01/dubious-role-of-bilderberg-club-created.html</span></span><br />\n<br />\n<div style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif;\">\n<span style=\"color: red; font-size: large;\">IN SANATANA DHARMA , NO WOMAN CAN ENTER ANY TEMPLE , WHEN SHE IS MENSTRUATING.. font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\">Steam and water feeds an iron fire due to oxidation of iron. Temperatures are&gt;1100 deg C<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\">Steam feeds Hydrogen fire. Both H2 and CO are combustible. Temperatures are &gt;1000 deg C<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\">Alkaline MECYL contributes Calcium Sulphates and Calcium Carbonates which cause stickiness in gilled tubes . Boiler exh gas outlet temperature should be &gt;165 deg C as condensation of H2SO4 in the exhaust gas makes the soot sticky.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\">Gas velocity in the boiler , circ water flow velocity and gas temperature on tube surface must NOT be too low.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\">Use preheated feed water of&gt;140C during start up.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\">Above is not applicable to smoke tube EGE who have self cleaning effect provided gas velocity is &gt; 20 metres / sec. Soot fires never cause any damage as tubes are surrounded by water.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"color: blue; font-size: 12.0pt;\"><br />\n</span></i></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"tab-stops: .5in;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12pt;\"></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\"><i style=\"color: blue;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp; &nbsp;</i>&nbsp;<span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"background-color: yellow;\">BOILERS</span><o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">An efficient boiler is one of the most sought after items on a parcel chemical tanker. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">With insufficient / bad quality steam , the cargo work efficiency suffers. Frustrating&nbsp; manhours are wasted by the deck team when tankcleaning water jet pressures and temperatures do NOT match to optimum for high MP cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">If the boiler steam gives high chlorides it is not of much use on deck when wall wash tests have to be done for cargoes like MEG Fibre grade where UCC requires a pass limit of 0.249 ppm chlorides. Or if the stainless steel maindeck ,steam inlet lines are constantly being fed free iron from the ungalvanised mild steel engine room steam pipes. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">There is a siphoning drum attached to the return main steam line on deck near the bridge front. This has a glass port for checking the top water level ----<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">Floating oils/ insoluble light density chemicals, <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">A drain to check high density insoluble chemicals which sink in water , or for soluble cargo sampling<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">A vent to check odour of water soluble clear cargoes / volatile gases. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">This engine room entry check of return condensate is vital, the chief engineer is also encouraged to use this engine room entry check point, where he can use his sense of smell. By the time the water enters the hotwell it is a bit too late to use the sense of smell.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%; mso-fareast-font-family: BatangChe;\">The return water must NOT be send to the engine room inspection chamber/ atmospheric condenser/ hotwell unless the deck siphoning drum contents have been passed by Chief officer. This responsibility cannot be delegated or abdicated by Chief officer. Failure to follow this vital Goodwood instruction may mean boiler explosion or off hire due to boiler tubes getting coated with cargo.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If viscous chemicals enter the boiler, the boiler will be destroyed due to overheating of the furnace caused by water carry over/ reduced water flow and reduced heat transfer. Particles floating on hotwell / cascade tank surface can be absorbed by absorbents like loofa sponges.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Steam flexible hoses should be immediately disconnected after steam blow into cargo pipelines and connected back at manifold or elsewhere ONLY when required.\u2014or you will have cargo entering the boiler. This applies to air blow flexible hoses and nitrogen hoses too. The entire deck force must be absolutely clear about this. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The deck steam max pressure is 7 bars. Quite often the shore&nbsp; steam blow is 10 bars (or higher). You could have cargo entering the boiler hotwell at a differential pressure of 3 bars if the ship/ shore hoses are open simultaneously , considering intermediate cargo valve seats are do not give&nbsp; perfect&nbsp; seal with high MP cargoes in low ambient temperatures.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">With insufficient boiler drum blow down or surface scum blow the steam arriving on deck may have water carry over which severely affect cargo discharge operations say of high MP cargoes in freezing weather.&nbsp; <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Funnel sparks must be avoided . The funnel must be monitored after an economizer wash. It is Chief engineers responsibility to advise the Master/ Chief Officer when economizer has been washed in port, so that sparks from the funnel in day time can be taken care of by relative wind. &nbsp;Excess MECYL feed on new ships and during long manoeverings can cause soot build up in economisers.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">If&nbsp; sparks are emitted from the funnel the tanker should, if necessary, alter course as soon as possible to avoid sparks falling on the tank deck. Sparks cannot be seen in daytime and during dep port pilotage course cannot be altered for favourable relative wind without the pilot reporting this matter. In standard ports there are official forums to report such incidents. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Remember safety first .Any cargo, ballasting or tank cleaning operations that are taking place must be immediately stopped and all tank openings closed<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">There are toxic cargoes like PHENOL where the return steam coil water must not be sent back to engine room hotwell . In such cases the TCFW is heated by the butterworth heater inside the pumproom and injected into the tank steam coils and returned back to the same TCFW tank as a continious closed loop. Portable adaptor manifolds will be available for fixed steam inlet/ return manifolds. &nbsp;<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><b><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">ECONOMISER WASHING:<o:p></o:p></span></b></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">E</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">n</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">g</span><span Off</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">ic</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">e</span>r<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\"> </span>to<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>B<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">oo</span>k.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin-top: 2.95pt;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">\u00a8<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">Off</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">ic</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;\">e</span>r<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">o</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>t<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">h</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">b</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">r</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">id</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">g</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\"> </span>to<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">re</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">co</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">r</span>d<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>t<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">h</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\"> </span>sh<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">ip\u2019</span>s <span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">p</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">o</span>s<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">i</span>t<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">i</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">o</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>a<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">n</span>d<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">t</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">i</span>me <span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">o</span>f <span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">co</span>m<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">pl</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">t</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">io</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">i</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>the De<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">c</span>k <span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">L</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">o</span>g<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">B</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">oo</span>k<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Ensure that there is no cargo/ oil contamination on the water side. Economisers must be kept clear of soot which lower efficiency during carriage of heating cargoes. Avoid using shore fresh water in boiler, always try and use fresh water generated on board. Shore water will usually contain excess chlorides , humous particles and silica. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Washing must be done by copious flow of hot water and not by atomizing high pressure cold wash from a kew machine, of couse you must check your holding tank capacity. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Open drains of turbocharger, exhaust manifold and exhaust boiler.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Make sure there is enough space in holding tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">During wash frequently check turbo charger and exhaust manifold drains to ensure no water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Carry out soot blowing after sailing. This soot blow must be monitored by chief engineer, to find out how efficient his staffs economizer washing efforts have been.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">After an economizer wash the soot keeps dropping. There must be a final collection of soot before boxing back casing covers. Or this soot will comes out as sparks on dep berth.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Routine boiler maintenance must be done.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">As a precaution against funnel fires and sparks; the burners, tubes, uptakes, exhaust manifolds and spark arresters should be maintained in good working condition. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Funnel uptakes, boiler tubes should be blown prior to arrival at and after departure from port. Boiler tubes should not be blown when the vessel is in port. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Boiler additives are chemicals which can affect the wall wash or deslopping contents for sensitive cargoes like Mono Ethylene Glycol fibre grade. Too muck alkali and you will be surprised to see that the chemical has turned a dark shade of red. Chief engineer must be made aware.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">The condensate from steam main steam inlet line must be tested to determine the chloride and free iron content. Remember free iron plastered on SS bulkheads can cause pitting or even polymerization. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">To prevent free iron on tank bulkheads and discolouration , before steaming tanks, &nbsp;boiler must be blown down. Waste some steam on deck, and don\u2019t be stingy about this. IMPORTANT\u2014 when you waste steam on deck or do live steaming the duty engineer must be told that water will have to be replenished in boiler, as the closed cycle is now open.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Always ensure that boiler feed water is fresh water generator output, when wall wash is looming ahead. Excess chlorides in feed water will cause lime deposits if not treated.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Engineering aspects\u2014<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Untreated boiler water has inherent salts and gases, which must be removed by chemicals or water softening chemicals. Salts cause scaling which reduce heat transfer. CO2 combines with water to form carbonic acid which attacks the boiler and condensation systems.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Oxygen in feed water causes severe corrosion and must be removed by thermal de-aeriation by keeping the feed water temp at around a practical value of 88 deg C. Around this temp CO2 is also removed.&nbsp; Oxygen scavenging chemicals will remove the remaining quarter of Oxygen which&nbsp; cannot be removed by heating feed water.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Alkaline treatment can neutralise&nbsp; the effects of carbonic acid and also remove the salts which cause scale. Daily check feed and boiler water condition. Boiler water treatment programmes must strictly be followed. <o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before sensitive cargoes like MEG FG where pure steam is required in cargo tanks\u2014chemical dosing may have to be stopped as an exceptional case , but only after informing the master. Check for steam and water leaks daily.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 150%;\">It is Chief Engineers responsibility to ensure there is good quality/ quantity steam for cargo and tank cleaning operations and that the tank cleaning heater is absolutely efficient.<o:p></o:p></span></div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><br />\n</div><div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 11pt; letter-spacing: 0.05pt; line-height: 150%;\">T</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 11pt; letter-spacing: -0.05pt; line-height: 150%;\">h</span><span style=\"font-family: 'Times New Roman', serif; font-size: 11pt; line-height: 150%;\">e<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> b</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">o</span>il<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span>r f<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">e</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span>d<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">w</span>at<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span>r <span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">u</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">s</span>t <span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">b</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">k</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">ep</span>t cl<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">a</span>n<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>a<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">n</span>d<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span>f<span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">r</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">o</span>f <span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">co</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">n</span>tami<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">n</span>at<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">i</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">o</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">n</span>. &nbsp;<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">S</span>al<span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">i</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">n</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">o</span>m<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span>t<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">e</span>rs <span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">m</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">u</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">s</span>t <span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">b</span>e<span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\">us</span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .1pt;\">e</span>d<span style=\"letter-spacing: -.05pt;\"> </span><span style=\"letter-spacing: .05pt;\">o</span>n<span I have visited Dwaraka 32 years ago and convinced myself that the &nbsp;ancient city extends to the sea and has been rebuilt 7 times , as per legend.&nbsp; 5 years after this I was vindicated when I saw &nbsp;Indian National TV Doordarshan showing underwater picture of these 7 stages .</span></span><br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Now let me introduce Macaulay, the great white liar . </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br />\n</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">He was under instructions from the Pope to inject poison into Hinduism and the great Vedic culture and belittle it, beyond recognition. He used Mueller to achieve this end.&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">Vatican had realized that almost all European languages have similarities to Sanskrit. &nbsp;</span></span><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So instead of saying that the hand slapped the face , it was important to establish that the face slapped the hand. &nbsp;</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">It was necessary to make all believe in ridiculous Christian Chronology \u2013 that the world was created at 9 AM on 23<sup>rd</sup> Oct 4004 BC and the great flood with Noah and ark party was in 2500 BC. &nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">So the hoax of the great Aryan invasion into India sounded all right if it was dated to 1500 BC. </span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\">The fact remains that all ancient Indian civilisations ( rather even all world civilisations ) gave birth on river banks.&nbsp;&nbsp;</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; The Mahabharata clearly talks about the River Saraswati drying up. The mighty and perennial Saraswati river flowed from the Himalayan Glaciers to the Rann of Kutch where it emptied into the Arabian sea. Dwaraka of Lord Krishna was part of this civilization. Ganges was also flowing at that time into the Bay of Bengal.</span></span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; ALL CARBON DATING WILL BE YOUNGER BY AROUND 3000 YEARS ..<br />\n<br />\nMAHABHARATA HAPPENED 6000 YEARS AGO..<br />\n<br />\nIT IS LINKED TO RIVER SARASWATI DRYING UP-- NOT TO SOME BULLSHIT SOLAR ECLIPSE..<br />\n<br />\nTHERE WAS NO SOLAR ECLIPSE.<br />\n<br />\nThe Rig Veda written in 5000 BC explains the solar eclipse well. Panchavimsa Brahmana speaks of four different stages of an eclipse. It describes beautifully the changing colours during the solar eclipse.<br />\n<br />\nArjuna had sworn to kill Jayadratha before sunset failing which he will commit suicide. The Kaurava army was successful in keeping Arjuna away from Jayadratha and sunset was nearing.<br />\n<br />\nSo Lord Krishna sent his Sudarshana Chakra which is a scalar interferometry based spinning discus, which created an severe inversion in the atmosphere.<br />\n<br />\nThe atmospheric refraction reversed ,and the sun suddenly dipped below the visible horizon causing absolute darkness. At this time there was a mighty cheer among the Kaurava ranks and Jayadratha peered out of his tent.<br />\n<br />\nAs per the rules of Dharma Yuddha it is NOT possible to kill an enemy after sunset. As soon as Krishna saw Jayadratha he commanded Arjuna to behead him with an arrow and immediately restored the atmospheric refraction the usual way. The sun suddenly came up above the visible horizon.<br />\n<br />\nThis was NOT a solar eclipse. And hence a solar eclipse should NOT be used to date the Mahabharata war of 4000 BC. The modern HAARP plays around with the ionosphere and can make lenses out of it bypushing the layer out.<br />\n<br />\nA solar eclipse occurs when the moon gets directly or nearly directly between the sun and Earth, and the moon's shadow falls on us. A solar eclipse can occur only during a new moon.<br />\n<br />\nIN MAHABHARATA , THE FINAL BATTLE BETWEEN DURYODANA AND BHIMA TOOK PLACE IN A STAGNANT WATER POOL , WITH BOTH KRISHNA AND BALARAMA WITH A GIANT PLOUGH OVER HIS SHOULDERS WATCHING.<br />\n<br />\nBHIMA FALSELY ACCUSED DURYODHANA OF HIDING IN THE POOL-- TO WHICH DURYODHANA ANGRILY SAID, THAT HE WAS JUST TRYING TO COOL DOWN HIS INDIGNATION, AT THE FOUL WAR TACTICS USED BY KRISHNA<br />\n<br />\nBALARAMA HAS JUST DIVERTED THE SARASWATI RIVER INTO GANGA -- USING HIS PLOUGH. font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. Ajit Vadakayil</a></cite><span class=\"icon user blog-author\" style=\"background-image: url(&quot;data:image/png; background-repeat: no-repeat; display: inline-block; font-weight: bold; height: 18px; margin: 0px 0px -4px 6px; width: 18px;\"></span><span class=\"datetime secondary-text\" style=\"margin-left: 6px;\"><a href=\"https://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2018/08/comments-overflow-for-inoperative-load.html?showComment=1535264994347#c2766037549176043609\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">August 26, 2018 at 11:59 AM</a></span></div>\n<div class=\"comment-content\" id=\"bc_0_57MC\" style=\"margin-bottom: 8px; text-align: justify;\">\nSOMEONE ASKED ME --<br />\n<br />\nWAS SARASWATI RIVER A MORE HOLY RIVER THAN GANGES<br />\n<br />\nYES!<br />\n<br />\nAYURVEDA USED SARASWATI RIVER WATER BEFORE THE RIVER WENT DRY..<br />\n<br />\nSARASWATI RIVER HAD AXOLOTLS<br />\n<br />\nhttp://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2011/01/mother-of-all-civilisations-saraswati.html<br />\n<br />\nGANGES RIVER HAS MACROPHAGES<br />\n<br />\nhttp://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2014/06/ganga-manthan-cleaning-of-river-ganges.html<br />\n<br />\nAxolotl is a species of aquatic salamander. Unlike humans, it has the \u201csuperpower\u201d of regenerating its limbs, spinal cord, heart, and other organs..<br />\n<br />\nYoung frogs are known to regrow limbs, though they lose this ability when they change from tadpoles to adult frogs. On the other hand, the axolotl retains it throughout its entire life, making it unique among vertebrates<br />\n<br />\nHumans have also been known to regenerate the tips of the fingers, including the bone and skin. I once lost the tip of my left forefinger on the ship--it has regrown fully.<br />\n<br />\nBECAUSE OF CHEMICAL POLLUTION FOR TANNERIES, GANGES MACROPHAGES HAVE LOST THEIR ANCIENT POWERS OF REGENERATION..<br />\n<br />\nInjecting a drug to get rid of macrophages in an axolotl\u2019s limb before amputation leads to the accumulation of scar tissue instead of regrowth..<br />\n<br />\nThis scarring, which happens when a protein called collagen becomes disordered, is a normal part of wound healing in humans, but it is unusual in axolotls. This result suggests that macrophages are essential for regeneration<br />\n<br />\nAxolotls stay 'babies' for their whole lives. Axolotls are neotenic creatures meaning they achieve sexual maturity without losing any of their larval features<br />\n<br />\nIf an axolotl is given a shot of iodine, it will experience a rush of hormones that triggers the animal's growth processes, and it will \"grow up\" and resemble a mature tiger salamander, their closest relative.<br />\n<br />\nHowever, this is not the axolotl's natural state. \"Grown-up\" axolotls are typically listless and die about a year after the injection.<br />\n<br />\nAxolotls can regenerate pretty much any body part. A number of amphibians are capable of regenerating limbs, but axolotls take this habit up a notch by regenerating jaws, spinal cords, skin and even portions of their brain. Axolotls can also receive organ transplants and will not reject the new organ.<br />\n<br />\nAxolotls have a genome 10 times the size of the human genome..<br />\n<br />\nhttps://www.youtube.com/watch?v=B0GJOjfYn74<br />\n<br />\ncapt ajit vadakayil<br />\n..</div>\n</div>\n</li>\n</ol>\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span>\n<br />\n<span style=\"line-height: 150%;\"><span class=\"Apple-style-span\" style=\"font-family: &quot;times&quot; , &quot;times new roman&quot; , serif;\"><br /></span></span>\n<br />\n<div class=\"avatar-image-container\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; float: left; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin: 0.2em 0px 0px; max-height: 36px; overflow: hidden; width: 36px;\">\n<img src=\"https://3.bp.blogspot.com/-0Gvy5mBcipE/WlAJZNfU3zI/AAAAAAABXsU/wZaBJr4cOoclmnshY0dz6Y3NbokDpLaaACK4BGAYYCw/s35/*\" style=\"border: 1px solid rgb(238, 238, 238); max-width: 36px;\" /></div>\n<div class=\"comment-block\" id=\"c782687426727886869\" style=\"background-color: #cccccc; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, FreeSerif, serif; font-size: 16px; margin-left: 48px; position: relative;\">\n<div class=\"comment-header\" id=\"bc_0_188M\" kind=\"m\" style=\"margin: 0px 0px 8px;\">\n<cite class=\"user blog-author\" style=\"font-style: normal; font-weight: bold;\"><a href=\"https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654\" rel=\"nofollow\" style=\"color: #888888; text-decoration-line: none;\">Capt. THIS IS RIVER WATER PLUS SILT.<br />\n<br />\n<b><span style=\"color: purple;\">SILT IS NOT JUST MUD--- IT IS THE COLLOIDAL LIFE OF THE RIVER..</span></b><br />\n<br />\n<b><span style=\"color: magenta;\">GANGES WATER AT GAUMUKH ( SOURCE ) CONTAINS MASSIVE AMOUNT OF COLLOIDAL SILVER AND OTHER COLLOIDS..</span></b><br />\n<br />\nTHIS WATER IS HIGHLY ALKALINE AND HAS AN EXTRAORDINARY AMOUNT OF HYDROGEN WITH AN EXTRA ELECTRON TO NEUTRALIZE DAMAGING FREE RADICALS WHICH CAUSE DNA DAMAGE AND RAPID AGEING.<br />\n<br />\nTHIS LOW SURFACE TENSION WATER IS BIO-ENERGISED MIRACLE WATER..LESS THAN THE USUAL 73 DYNES..<br />\n<br />\nTHIS MIRACLE WATER EASILY PENETRATES THE 75 TRILLION CELLS AND MITOCHONDRIAL MEMBRANES TO SUPPLY NUTRIENTS AND FLUSH WAY TOXINS.<br />\n<br />\nIN THE OLYMPICS CERTAIN ATHLETES HAVE GOOD COACHES WHO TELL THEM WHAT TO DRINK BEFORE THE RACE.<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2016/09/marathon-running-secrets-of.html<br /><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2016/09/marathon-running-secrets-of_16.html<br /><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2016/09/marathon-running-secrets-of_17.html<br /><br />http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2016/09/marathon-running-secrets-of_17.html</span><br />\n<br />\nI WAS AT SEA FOR 40 YEARS AND THUS MISSED FAMILY MARRIAGES--WHERE RELATIVES MEET EACH OTHER..<br />\n<br />\nI WENT TO KANNUR TO GIVE INVITATIONS FOR MY ELDER SONs WEDDING 3 YEARS AGO..<br />\n<br />\nMOST OF MY RELATIVES WERE SEEING ME AFTER HALF A CENTURY.. AND THEY ALL MADE SURE THAT I ATE WHATEVER NATIVE SWEETS THEY GAVE ME --IN ADDITION TO SWEET COLD DRINKS AND SWEET TEA..<br />\n<br />\nON THE DRIVE BACK FROM KANNUR TO CALICUT MY TOES AND FINGERS WENT HAYWIRE.. I BANGED INTO A MOTORCYCLIST AT A TRAFFIC LIGHT.. HE JUST LOOKED BACK AND ACTED AS IF NOTHING HAPPENED.<br />\n<br />\nI WAS UNABLE TO EVEN HOLD THE WHEEL LEAVE ALONE PRESS THE BRAKE.<br />\n<br />\nI IMMEDIATELY TOLD MY WIFE-- I WILL PARK AT THE NEAREST BAKERY-- MY BODY NEEDS SODIUM AND POTASSIUM IMMEDIATELY.. BUY A TIN OF SALTED CASHEW..BEFORE I GET BRAIN FOG..<br />\n<br />\nIT WAS 2130 PM AND MOST STORES WERE SHUTTING..<br />\n<br />\nMY WIFE CAME RUNNING BACK WITH A HUGE TIN OF SALTED CASHEW--I GORGED ON IT AND DRANK LOT OF WATER...<br />\n<br />\nWITHIN THREE MINUTES I WAS OK--AND I DROVE THE NEXT ONE HOUR TO CALICUT AT FULL SPEED WITHOUT PROBLEM..<br />\n<br />\n<span style=\"color: red;\">https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=_bPFKDdWlCg</span><br />\n<br />\nBONGS CANT GET HILSA FISH ANYMORE AFTER THE FARAKKA ARRAGE WAS BUILT SANS FISH LADDER..
